Aid Wang Directorate Holds General Meeting of All Circles in Zhabei Yesterday, Resolves to Petition the Municipal Government 163

The Directorate of All Circles in Zhabei Aiding Wang Binyan for Publicly Caused Troubles held a general meeting of representatives of local gentry and merchants in Zhabei at the Grand Auditorium of the Zhabei Charity Group at 2:00 PM yesterday. Over a hundred people attended, with Tang Youwei as chairman and Wang Yiheng as recorder. The chairman reported on the previous meeting's minutes, proposals, and documents. Wang's bankruptcy due to public affairs is imminent, and the people of Zhabei should unite and provide practical assistance. Then the following was discussed: How to deal with the court's implementation of the auction of Wang's property? Resolution: All circles should provide practical assistance pending the auction date. How to claim debts from the government? Resolution: Forty representatives will be recommended to petition Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, and Wang Xiaolai, and then petition the municipal government to request prompt relief. Call for justice for the Guangdong Bank, the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Federation, and others. Recommendation of the petition delegation. Resolution: She Xipin, Li Guangzhen, Wei Zhiqiu, Cai Qiajun, Qu Jisheng, Situ Yi, Jiang Zhongliang, Tang Youwei, Zhou Linfeng, Wang Maoqing, and Yu Shaotang will be recommended to lead all attendees to go. Organization of a creditor group. Resolution: Retained. The draft letter of presentation is recorded on the left.

Presentation to the Municipal Government

We respectfully report that the case of Wang Binyan's Jiangzhe垫欵, which was caused by public affairs, was previously submitted by the local public group to the municipal government requesting relief. We are deeply grateful that your seat has approved the method to maintain it. However, it has not yet been granted, and our expectations are even deeper. Wang Binyan has been in Shanghai for more than thirty years, and has always devoted his loyalty and sacrificed everything for local public welfare and the happiness and security of the people. During the various wars, he always focused on maintaining the locality. Therefore, Zhabei has been able to turn danger into safety and suffer no losses, which is not an exaggeration of our people. For example, during the January 28th Incident, Wang also maintained the locality for more than thirty days, patrolling day and night, and maintaining it in every way. Although there were petty thefts, the society was still quiet. This is due to Wang's presence. We are deeply grateful for this. Today, Wang is suffering from public affairs, even to the point of bankruptcy. First, the property was seized, and then auctioned off. It is tense every day and pressing every step. Once auctioned, he will have nowhere to go. In addition to our people benefiting, our conscience has not disappeared. Therefore, we specially jointly petition your seat. If Wang's property is auctioned off, it will be tantamount to abandoning the protection of our people. Your seat has always been extremely kind and regards the citizens of Zhabei as children. How can you bear to put their nanny to death? Abandoning Wang is abandoning the people. Now, we boldly present our request and respectfully ask your seat to quickly consult the court to postpone the auction. At the same time, we request your government to temporarily垫欵 84,000 yuan to clear the lawsuits. The money will be repaid by the original debtors of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, or the original contract will be mortgaged, and your government will collect it from the citizens and use it for the citizens. This is also a matter of common sense and reason. If your seat gives a promise, everything will be resolved. The amount is only 84,000 yuan, not all of it, and it is easier to implement. We also ask you to show mercy to our foolish sincerity, and those who are grateful will not be just Wang alone. If we are blessed with a promise, Zhabei will be fortunate, and the merchants and people will be fortunate. We respectfully present this to Wu, Mayor of Shanghai.

Letter to Yu, Du, and Wang: We respectfully inform you that Mr. Wang's case has been discussed with Minister Kong, who agreed to present it to the Ministry of Finance and then to the municipal government for subsidy. This is all due to your public's great assistance and enthusiasm for public welfare. We are deeply grateful. However, the municipal government must be troubled again to have a thorough consultation with the mayor, so that it can be effective. This case has been in litigation for many years, and success or failure depends on this one action. We ask you to use your influence to bring the matter to fruition from beginning to end. Not only will Mr. Wang be cleared of the lawsuit, but the local people will also be grateful to no end. We hereby express our thanks and wish you a speedy progress.

Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society Organizes Petty Savings Association for Members 167

The Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society, in view of the fact that registered rickshaw pullers generally do not save money and suffer from food shortages when business is slow, has decided to organize a petty savings association for members in the society's various meeting places in order to encourage members to save. The procedures are simple and the interest rates are generous. The purpose is to enable rickshaw pullers to save a little from their daily income after deducting daily legitimate expenses. Therefore, the savings amount is set at a minimum of one cent in silver dollars, and the monthly savings amount should not exceed five yuan. For savings of less than 50 yuan, the interest rate is one cent per month. The method for exceeding 50 yuan will be determined separately. All members who join the savings association will be given a passbook. The withdrawal of savings will be based on the member's rickshaw license and seal. It is understood that this kind of savings association is a pioneering initiative in the country. The accumulation of small amounts into large sums is quite interesting. It is expected that the total number of registered rickshaw pullers in Shanghai is over 40,000, and the number of participants will be very enthusiastic.

Japanese Expert of Chinese Medicine Gives a Lecture at the Chinese Medical College 171

Mr. Imai Toyokumo, President of the Osaka Kampo Medical College in Japan, is deeply versed in Chinese medical prescriptions and has gained considerable insight. He arrived in Shanghai by ship from Osaka a few days ago. Yesterday, he gave a lecture at the Chinese Medical College on North Henan Road and Old Bazizi Road. He arrived at 2:00 PM and was received by the college's President Xue Wenyuan and Guo Boliang. He exchanged medical opinions with the college's Dean Jiang Wenfang, stating briefly that since the Meiji Restoration in Japan, Chinese medicine has been abandoned, but now the government and the public are becoming increasingly averse to Western medicine injections and are respecting Chinese medicine and Chinese herbal remedies. He has established a Kampo Medical College and a Chinese herbal medicine garden in Osaka for practical research. He deeply admires the reputation of your esteemed college in the Orient and has come specifically to visit and conduct research, etc. He then proceeded to the college's auditorium to give a lecture and practical demonstration on the four diagnostic methods. More than 300 people attended. He described the importance of the twelve meridians in Chinese medicine for treatment and the efficacy of Chinese herbal medicines, stating that their effectiveness and miraculous cures surpass Western medicine. People in the Orient have awakened from their error and, in the near future, the position of Chinese medicine will inevitably return to what it was sixty years ago, etc. After the lecture, Dean Jiang led a tour of the college's achievements, which he greatly praised. He said that after returning to Japan, he plans to send students to study at the college for exchange. He took a photograph at 5:00 PM and left the college.

Shanghai Municipal Council Wharf Crane Rental Regulations 173

The Shanghai Municipal Council wharves in Hongkou Huishan and Yangshupu have several cranes available for rent by passengers and merchants. The rental fee is based on weight, ranging from 15 cents per lift for loads not exceeding half a ton to seven dollars per lift for loads not exceeding seven and a half tons. The minimum charge is one dollar and forty cents. During non-working hours and on Sundays, a surcharge of half the fee is applied. Those wishing to rent these cranes should first notify the Roads Department of the Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council in writing (office room 232). Office hours are from 6:00 AM to 11:00 AM and 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM from April to October, and from 7:00 AM to 11:30 AM and 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM from November to March.

Detective Qian Chenglong and Detectives Zhang Ziying and Xia Zhenglong of the French Concession Police learned that someone was secretly producing the narcotic drug morphine for profit at No. 3 Huishun Lane, 525 Min'guo Road, outside the Small North Gate. Therefore, at about 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, they went to the address with the Western Inspector and detectives on duty to search it secretly. They only found the bookkeeper Zhu Guangzhao (27 years old, Ningbo native) and the old steward Xu Zhengxiang (54 years old, Ningbo native). Raw materials for manufacturing narcotics of considerable value were seized. However, the main suspects, the engineer and workers, had already fled upon hearing the news and remain at large. The detectives took the two suspects Zhu and Xu, along with the evidence, back to the police station. They sent detectives to guard the premises and ordered detectives to investigate and arrest the main suspects who were at large to bring them to justice for interrogation. According to the confessions of the two suspects, Zhu and Xu, the boss of the organization has already passed away. The Police Department is now conducting a thorough investigation. The two suspects who were apprehended will be sent to court for trial today.

Kidnapping of Zhou Chunbo's Son: Kidnappers Receive Sentences; Wang Xie'shi Acquitted and Released on Bail 176

Zhou Chunbo, a native of Hubei who resides at No. 135 Pobo Lane, Luban Road, in the French Concession and works as a broker at the Cloth Exchange, had his four-year-old son, Jiasheng, kidnapped at 2:00 PM on April 4 of this year by the hired female servant Jin Zhou'shi. A ransom of 50,000 yuan was demanded in a letter. The police were notified, and Inspector Jin Jiulin, Detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhong Dongchang, and Dai Rongji of the French Concession Police Department rescued the hostage on April 17 inside No. 12 Peide Lane, Yangjia Village, Pudong. They successively arrested the kidnappers Jin Hongxiang, Xu Rengui, Zhang Xibiao, Xi Xinquan, Wang Shipin, Ma Liangfu, Zhu Mingji, Chen Jianzhao, Jin Zhou'shi, Wang Xie'shi, and suspects Lu Zhenwu, Zhao Jin'shi, Wang Xiangzhen, and Wang Xiangzhao, a total of thirteen men and women. They confiscated one box cannon and seventeen lead bullets and sent them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. It was found that Lu Zhenwu's suspicion was lighter, and the court ordered him to be released on bail. Zhao Jin'shi, Wang Xiangzhao, and Wang Xiangzhen were found to have no involvement and were released. The Police Department prosecuted the remaining defendants according to law. Judge Zhang Chaozuo held repeated hearings and appointed lawyers Wang Shizong and Wang Liangqing, etc., to provide free legal defense for the defendants. The announcement was concluded and a date was set for sentencing. The details have already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. Judge Zhang presided over the First Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to be brought to court. After briefly questioning their ages and origins, he sentenced Xu Rengui to fifteen years of imprisonment and fifteen years of deprivation of civil rights. Zhang Xibiao and Jin Hongxiang were each sentenced to ten years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights. Chen Jianzhao was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment and eight years of deprivation of civil rights. Wang Shipin was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment and seven years of deprivation of civil rights. Ma Liangfu and Xi Xinquan were each sentenced to five years of imprisonment and five years of deprivation of civil rights. Jin Zhou'shi was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment and four years of deprivation of civil rights. One pistol and seventeen lead bullets were confiscated. Wang Xie'shi was acquitted. Wang Xie'shi was allowed to be released on bail of 1,000 yuan during the appeal period, with a shopkeeper as guarantor, to be available whenever summoned. The remaining defendants were detained in the prison.

Trafficking of a Married Woman: Accidentally Encountered Xu Xin'da and Others 177

Huang Ziliang, a 31-year-old carpenter from Pudong, married a wife, Shen'shi, who was 32 years old and quite beautiful. They lived together in Lan'nidu, Pudong. In November of last year, his old friends Xu Xin'da and Wang Gu'shi came to visit and invited Huang's wife, Shen'shi, to go to Shanghai to see a play. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Shanghai, they took Shen'shi to Zhenru and sold her to Di, who lives at No. 15 Di'jia Bridge, to be his wife. After dividing the money, they disappeared without a trace. When Huang saw that Xu and the others did not return, he suspected something was wrong and came to Shanghai to inquire. After several months, he was informed by his friend Chen Buxian that Xu Xin'da and Wang Gu'shi were hiding at No. 371, Route Ghisi Fel, West Shanghai. Huang went with Chen. When they arrived near Wujiaochang, Caojiadu, they accidentally encountered Xu and Wang face to face. Huang immediately grabbed Xu and reported him to the policeman on duty there, who took them to the Caojiadu Public Security Branch. Xu and Wang confessed to trafficking a married woman. Based on their confessions, the branch sent detectives to Di'jia Bridge, together with the local police, to bring Shen'shi back. The branch, considering that the case involved trafficking a married woman, prepared a document to send all three to the General Bureau for investigation and verification.

Railway Parcel Transport Fees: Revised to be Charged According to Actual Weight: To Be Implemented from June 1 of This Year 181

According to reliable information from the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, the Ministry of Railways believes that the current railway parcel transport rates, where light but bulky items are calculated based on volume converted to kilograms, impose an excessive burden on merchants. Therefore, it has ordered all railways to abolish the method of calculating one kilogram for every three cubic decimeters of volume and to uniformly change to charging based on actual weight. It is stipulated that this will be implemented from June 1 of this year. The revised parcel transport rates are listed below: Within 250 kilometers: 7 cents; From 251 kilometers to 500 kilometers to 750 kilometers, or less than 50 kilometers: 3.75 cents; From 751 kilometers onwards: 2.5 cents. The minimum transport fee for parcels, whether on this railway or in conjunction with other railways, is set at 20 cents per item. Parcel weight will be calculated in increments of one kilogram. Any fractional weight less than one kilogram will be counted as one kilogram.

Murder Case on Chongqing Road: Body Examined Yesterday: Knife Wounds and Strangulation Marks Found: Confirmed to Be the Brother of the Owner of Gao He Shoe Store 182

The body found murdered in the kitchen of No. 13 Ma'an Lane, Chongqing Road, was transported to the Forensic Examination Institute on Fielun Road. Yesterday morning, the Procuratorate of the First Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Tang Peiyou, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan, to conduct an examination. As a result, knife wounds were found on both cheeks of the body, and strangulation marks were found on the neck. It was confirmed that the deceased was indeed murdered during his lifetime. It was also proven that the deceased was Huang Futian, the younger brother of Huang Fuchao, the owner of the Gao He Women's Shoe Store at No. 191 Tongfu Road. Huang Futian left on a bicycle on the afternoon of the 16th of this month in response to a customer's phone call to deliver goods and has not returned since. A report had been filed with the Police Department at the time. The identity of the body was filled in, and Prosecutor Tang ordered the deceased's brother, Huang Fuchao, to claim the body for burial and ordered the Police Department to arrest the murderer to investigate the cause of the murder.

Conspiracy to Defraud 50,000 Gold: Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Accuses Zheng Dengqing and Zhang Bofang of Forgery, etc.: Zheng Dengqing and Others Impersonated Chairman Yu Zuoting's Name to Extort 50,000 from Shanghai Textile Printing and Dyeing Company - Trial Opened Yesterday, Both Defendants Claimed Illness and Did Not Appear - 183

Zheng Dengqing, an executive member of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, colluded with Zhang Boyan, a dismissed employee of the association, to forge documents of investigation issued by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and falsely signed the name of Chairman Yu Zuoting, plotting to defraud the Shanghai Textile Printing and Dyeing Company of 50,000 gold. This was reported by the company's General Manager Zhang Rongchu, and it involved Executive Members Wang and Lu of the Chamber of Commerce. The situation was very serious for a time. The incident was heard by the authorities of the National Government, who immediately conducted an investigation. As for the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce itself, in addition to convening emergency meetings of all executive and supervisory members, based on the forged documents provided by the informant and Zheng's confession, they resolved to dismiss Zheng Dengqing's position as executive

committee member to maintain discipline. With respect to Zheng and Zhang, it was deemed that they had violated criminal law. were Japanese goods, and notified Zhang Rongchu. Suspecting a One-Dollar Reward: Indian Constable Shoots and Kills Cousin: Armstrong Took Revenge; Hang Baoshan Was Also Shot 184

An Indian named Avv Baggu Guansheng, 35 years old, has been serving as a gatekeeper at the China Industrial Bank at No. 130 Beijing Road in the Public Concession for more than ten years. He is extremely kind and conscientious in his work, so he is deeply trusted by the bank. Moreover, the bank's director, Gong Xinchan, also pitied his hardship, and always gave him rewards whenever he came to Shanghai. Five years ago, Avv Baggu Guansheng, because his cousin Armstrong had been unemployed for a long time and was on the verge of starvation, pleaded with the bank to arrange for him to be employed. He was allowed to be employed and was also assigned to be a gatekeeper, alternating between day and night shifts with Avv, receiving a monthly salary of 35 yuan. Unexpectedly, once Armstrong's livelihood was secured, he suddenly resumed his old habits, constantly seeking trouble and quarreling with others. He even drank excessively and looked for trouble for no reason, so that those who associated with Armstrong were all afraid of him like a tiger and rushed to Avv to complain. Avv repeatedly advised Armstrong at the time, but Armstrong not only did not listen but even regarded Avv as an enemy. However, Avv remained the same as before, being kind and considerate. The day before yesterday, the bank's chairman, Gong Xinchan, came to Shanghai from Tianjin and gave Avv Baggu Guansheng two paper dollars as a reward. Avv immediately gave one paper dollar to Armstrong and told him its source. Unexpectedly, because the previous rewards were always two yuan per person, Armstrong suspected that Avv had deliberately embezzled the other half, so he held a grudge. At about 4:00 AM yesterday morning, he secretly carried a water pipe and rushed into Avv's bedroom. Avv was sleeping soundly and had not yet woken up when he struck Avv's head hard. Avv's skull was pierced, and his brain matter spilled out, and he died immediately. However, Armstrong was still afraid that he was not dead and struck another blow, which happened to hit another Indian constable who was in the same bed on his right foot. He woke up in pain and saw Armstrong standing by the bed with a hideous look. He was greatly frightened and jumped out of bed and ran out. Armstrong thought that it was Avv Baggu Guansheng, so he chased after him. Unexpectedly, the doorway of Avv's bedroom happened to be the sleeping place of Hang Baoshan (37 years old), a Yangzhou native who was the bank's cook. At that time, he had been awakened by the commotion and was about to get out of bed to peep when Armstrong stepped out of Avv's room and saw Hang standing at the doorway. Thinking that he was coming to stop him, he also struck him with the iron pipe. He was hit and his scalp was broken, and blood flowed like a fountain. He immediately fainted, and Avv still continued to chase after another constable, all the way to Beijing Road and Bowu Yuan Road. Fortunately, at that time, a Western constable happened to be patrolling there, and another Indian constable ran to inform him of the whole story. The Western constable arrested Armstrong and took him to the police station. They reported to the British Consulate and requested them to send someone to investigate. The body of Avv Baggu Guansheng was transported to the forensic examination institute for examination. The injured constable and Hang Baoshan were also treated in the hospital afterward. The murderer Armstrong has been transferred to the British Consulate for legal action.

Two Heads in a Small Coffin: Not Murder Victims, but the Skulls of Two Children 185

At about 10:40 PM the night before last, a red small coffin containing two human heads, resembling a boy and a girl, was discovered in a deserted area on Jiaotong Road, Zhabei. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It has now been verified that these human heads were not those of murdered victims. One was the skull of a four- or five-year-old boy who had died of illness, and the other was thought to be the skull of a three- or four-year-old girl of superstitious parents. A small coffin and a rush mat bag containing a corpse were discarded there a few days ago. The corpse was subsequently gnawed on by stray dogs, leaving only one head. Someone intended to move it into the small coffin, but when they opened the coffin lid, another head suddenly appeared. In a state of panic, they spread the word to the neighboring alleys, leading to a false rumor that they were the heads of a murdered boy and girl. Yesterday, the charity organization sent workers to remove and bury them.

The Public Concession Authority Encourages Birth Registration: Issues Colorful and Finely Printed Birth Reports to Certify Children's Age and Various Rights 186

Since the Shanghai Public Concession Authority has no regulations requiring the registration of births of Chinese residents in the concession, it is difficult to obtain accurate statistical reports. Recently, in order to encourage birth registration, the Public Health Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council has specially produced a colorful birth report, which is quite beautiful and pleasing to the eye. The design of this birth report is very much in line with the psychology of Chinese ladies. It features the sun, moon, stars, auspicious clouds, and two unicorns emerging from the clouds, which is in line with Du Fu's saying of a unicorn in the sky, as a premonition of the child's intelligence. On both sides stand young boys and girls, holding babies. Below is a magnificent building, resembling the scenery of the Bund, subtly reflecting the local scenery. Inside is the child's name, gender, date and place of birth, and the names, occupations, and addresses of the parents. From now on, all parents can register their child's birth at the nearest health branch and receive the colorful birth report signed and issued by the Statistics Section of the Public Health Department for a small fee of five cents. The birth reports of babies delivered by doctors registered with the Public Health Department can be directly obtained from the Statistics Section of the Public Health Department at No. 223 Hankou Road. Birth registration has long been implemented in various countries, and its benefits are approximately to prove age and origin, determine inheritance rights and various benefits related to age, such as school age, working age, marriage age, and age for holding public office. All parents who value their children's future interests should pay attention to this.

On Qimei Road: Patrol Police Arrest Two Robbers; One Robber Wounded by Gunfire 187

In the Qimei Road area of Zhabei, street robbery cases have been occurring frequently recently. Xu Wenlian, a resident of No. 6 Dexing Lane, Xiangyan Bridge Road, was walking home alone around 12 o'clock on the night of the 25th of this month. While passing Yangjia浜 Road, he suddenly noticed three robbers dressed in blue cloth short jackets following him closely. Fortunately, Xu was alert and avoided being assaulted. He paid close attention and, around 9:30 the night before last, spotted the same three robbers walking west along Qimei Road. Xu promptly reported this information to Patrol Officer Chen Lizhang at Post No. 5 of the Jixiang Road Sub-station. Officer Chen, along with Xu, followed them, observing their actions. The three robbers noticed they were being followed and scattered, attempting to escape. One robber crossed Guanzhong Road and entered Runde Lane. Officer Chen chased after him and, when he caught up, the robber immediately fired three shots from a Mauser pistol. None of the bullets hit. Seeing the dangerous situation, Officer Chen drew his gun and fired six shots in return. One bullet hit the robber's upper right shoulder, entering through the chest and exiting through the back, causing profuse bleeding. He collapsed to the ground and was apprehended. The police seized a No. 50518, No. 3 Mauser pistol, loaded with two bullets, and discovered five more bullets, seven yuan in legal tender, a pawn ticket, and a copper watch in his pockets. Xu Wenlian also bravely stepped forward and subdued another robber, finding an iron axe on his person. Only one robber escaped into the crowd. The two apprehended robbers were taken to the Linping Road Police Station. The wounded robber was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. His injuries were severe, and he was unable to speak. He was identified as Wang A'gen, also known as [blank], from Yancheng. The other robber was interrogated by the Detective Squad of the Night Traffic North Station. He confessed to being Zhou Yulin, from Yancheng, 28 years old. He claimed that a fugitive named Li provided them with firearms, and he and Wang A'gen committed the crime on Qimei Road, leading to their arrest. Police detectives, accompanied by Zhou, attempted to apprehend Li, but were unsuccessful. The case was reported to the General Bureau as a case of armed gang robbery with intent, and the suspects were detained for questioning. Meanwhile, a strict search is underway for the remaining accomplices, with a view to their severe punishment.

According to the National Society, Fan Yan Clan is 35 years old and from Ningbo Cixi. Her husband, Fan A'hong, was a tailor who passed away in 1925. She has a 13-year-old daughter named [blank] Ju. As she has no one in her husband's family and is from a poor background, she returned to her maternal home after her husband's death. Central Machinery Factory: Factory Building Project Nearing Completion 189

The steel skeletons and scaffolding of the three factory buildings for the Central Machinery Factory in Beixinjing, including the machinery manufacturing, iron manufacturing, and steel manufacturing plants, have been completed as early as January and February of this year, since construction began last year. However, the lead roofing sheets only arrived from England in March, so construction of the roofing only began in April. After an inspection by the factory director, Lu Weipu, it was discovered that the inside of the lead sheets had not been painted. Consequently, they were dismantled last month and two layers of paint and primer were applied. They are currently being reinstalled and are expected to be completed in about half a month. The walls, windows, and new-style air vents on the roof of each factory have already been installed, providing excellent lighting and ventilation. The machinery for each factory has been gradually transported and placed inside the factory buildings. As soon as the factory buildings are completed, the machinery can be installed. In addition, there is also a seamless pipe factory, for which bidding has already been opened, but the winning bid has not yet been announced. When completed, its scope will be larger than the three existing factories.

Over a Thousand Bean Curd Shops: Closed for Three Days Starting Yesterday 190

Public Association's Efforts to Persuade Shops Failed; Slight Price Increase to Maintain Operations Started on June 1st

Over a thousand bean curd shops in the city, including those in Nanshi, Zhabei, the city center, the Public Concession, the French Concession, Pudong, Huxi, and other areas, have been affected by the severance of soybean supplies due to the occupation of the four northeastern provinces. The price of soybeans, which used to be over six yuan per dan (a unit of weight), has now soared to over nine yuan, an increase of nearly one-third. This has made it difficult for shop owners to maintain their businesses. Consequently, they decided to raise prices on the 29th of last month, to be implemented on June 1st. Fearing that consumers would misunderstand, they voluntarily closed their shops for three days starting yesterday.

Public Association Issues Emergency Notice

The Public Association issued an emergency notice regarding the price increase: "Due to the soaring cost of raw materials and significant losses, a meeting of all member representatives was convened on the 29th of last month to revise the price list of all goods, effective June 1st. Circulars have been distributed to each household for compliance. However, it has recently been reported that some businesses intend to close their shops for three days before the price increase. Such abrupt closures are inappropriate. Furthermore, the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau has issued an order to all trade associations in the city stating that they may not close their shops without approval. We hereby solemnly declare that all businesses should not lightly close their shops, so as not to cause inconvenience. In addition to sending staff to persuade businesses, this notice is urgently issued as above."

Efforts to Persuade Shops Prove Ineffective

The closure of shops became a reality yesterday. Fearing misunderstanding, Association Chairman Tan Yueming, Standing Committee Members Qiu Senlin and Han Wenjun, and Secretary-General Shi Yizheng went to shops in Nanshi, Zhabei, Pudong, Huxi, and the two special districts to persuade them to resume business as usual. However, the shop owners remained firm in their attitude and refused to accept the advice. They will continue to close their shops today and tomorrow.

Price Increase on June 1st Definitely Implemented

The goods on the market yesterday were a portion of the stock available for market application. However, with no goods for sale, even stale and smelly bean curd was selling at triple the price in various small vegetable markets. There will be no goods available for sale today and tomorrow. It is reported that the industry has decided to implement the price increase starting June 1st. The prices will increase by about one-fifth. The detailed price list is omitted for brevity.

Prosecutor Appeals Pudong Gaoqiao Murder Case 193

Lu Zhiliang Released on 8,000 Yuan Shop Guarantee; Chen Huang Clan Remanded in Custody Without Bail

Chen Hongfu, a Chongming farmer from Yanjiachao, Gaoqiao, Pudong, was murdered on the night of November 27th of last year and his body was abandoned on the riverbank. The local保長 reported the incident to the local court for inspection. The deceased's wife, Chen Huang Clan, initially refused to have the body inspected, and later refused to appear. When prosecutor Li Fen of the court arrived for the inspection, the woman covered her face and showed no tears. Based on various circumstances, she was considered highly suspicious. At the same time, Lu Zhiliang, the deceased's maternal uncle, was in the midst of a lawsuit with the deceased, and the deceased was not well-behaved during his lifetime, so Lu was also considered suspicious. Both were taken into custody. A field investigation was conducted, and the local保長 reported that the deceased's children claimed that the deceased was murdered by Lu Zhiliang and Chen Huang Clan, who broke two of his ribs. After hearing the report, the prosecutor indicted Lu Zhiliang and Chen Huang Clan for murder. When Presiding Judge Cai Dingcheng reviewed the case, the children's statement was not made in court, and there was no other corroborating evidence. Moreover, the deceased was not well-behaved during his lifetime, so there may have been another murderer. Therefore, the judge declared the defendants not guilty. Lu Zhiliang was released on an 8,000 yuan shop guarantee, while Chen was remanded in custody without bail. Now, the original prosecutor has filed an appeal, stating that based on the past circumstances of the case, the defendants cannot escape suspicion. The prosecutor is requesting that the first instance judgment be corrected. The defendants will be sent to Suzhou for trial in the near future.

Guangchao Charity Hall in Fu'an Lane, Yongxing Road, Zhabei, has been established for over twenty years, dedicated to burying children's corpses and respecting written paper as its heavenly duty. All expenses are funded by donations from enthusiastic Chaozhou natives in Shanghai. The hall buries thousands of children's corpses each year, not only respecting humanity but also benefiting hygiene. The children's corpses received by the hall are sent to the Pushan Villa for burial. This year, the hall buried 394 children's corpses in January, 977 in February, 568 in March, and 480 in April. Since 1933, Lin Wenyi has received 1,000 bottles of Jizhong Water from the Shidezhi Factory each year, and Pengshoutang in Ximen has donated 7,000 bottles each year. These have been continuously donated for three years and transported by the hall to various charitable halls in Chaozhou and Shantou to distribute to the poor and sick in the countryside, saving countless lives. Its contribution is significant. The hall specially made two 6-foot mirror frames. Guo Jiuru, chairman of the Chaozhou Native Place Association in Shanghai, wrote "Extensive Beneficence and Assistance to All" and presented it to the Shidezhi Factory, and wrote "Happy to Do Good and Give to All" and presented it to Pengshoutang, thanking them on behalf of the poor and sick in Chaozhou and Shantou. On the 28th of this month, Chen Yubo, director of the hall, and Lin Wenyi and Xiao Kangshi personally sent them to the Shidezhi Factory and Pengshoutang to praise their merits.

* A letter was sent to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association to expand the scope of the association's publication to include news from the district branch associations of the Citizen's Federation. Passed.

* The Sanitary Department and Russian police of the French Concession often arbitrarily copy house numbers and impose unreasonable penalties, which should be strictly negotiated and corrected to alleviate the suffering of citizens. Passed.

* Police exercise the power to punish, obstructing legal rights. In the future, even if citizens violate police regulations, they should be transferred to the Second Special District Court for adjudication to ensure fairness. Passed.

* In the event of rental disputes among citizens in the district, the district branch associations should be informed first for fair mediation to avoid litigation. Passed.

* If citizens occasionally default on rent, water, and electricity bills, the French Concession Municipal Council and the water and electricity companies use cutting off water and electricity as a coercive measure, which should be negotiated and corrected. The example of the Public Concession Municipal Council prosecuting in the First Special District Court should be followed. Passed.

* Telephone charges are calculated by the call, and the counting is inaccurate. Actively oppose. Passed.

* Delegates were recommended to participate in the public memorial service for Mr. Hu Zhentang. Passed. Wu Guowei was recommended as the representative.

* Intensify publicity to expand the recruitment of citizens in the district to join the association, and focus on citizens in the neighborhoods during recruitment. Passed.

* Support the proposal of the Third District Branch Association that citizens in each district should request that the procedures of various agencies and organizations be effective only after being forwarded by the Municipal Federation Branch Associations of each relevant district. Passed.

* Thank the Leshan Temple for providing free housing as the association's premises. Passed. Handed over to the Executive Committee for handling.

* Based on the proportion of Chinese taxpayers, the French Consul should be requested to increase the number of Chinese directors in the Municipal Council, and the municipal government should be instructed to negotiate. Passed.

* A letter was sent to the Second Special District Court requesting attention to rental disputes and the implementation of mediation. Passed.

Weather Report 207

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and surrounding areas are hot with sandstorms and strong southwest to northwest winds due to a low-pressure system passing through Mongolia and moving eastward. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the Hankou area are cloudy with thunderstorms and northwest to northeast winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and this area are cloudy and gradually changing, with the possibility of rain and strong southeast winds due to a low-pressure system in Hunan. There is rain in the East China Sea and Taiwan with strong northeast winds. A small hurricane is passing southeast of Luzon and occasionally moving north. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was 73.6 degrees at the highest and 58.3 degrees at the lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 64.2 degrees and the lowest was 58.8 degrees.

Yesterday, Chih Chih and Fudan were strong in the field events, while Guanghua was strong in the track events. The competition will continue this afternoon with a total of ten events in the finals. The wind is gentle, and the climate is suitable, and the athletes from each school are in high spirits. Yesterday, there were three field events and four track events (preliminaries). As a result, Chih Chih and Fudan tied for first place in the field events with 15 points each, while Guanghua was in the lead in the track events with 17 points. Today's program has ten events and will start early at 1:30 PM. The track events are more important. 1 PM in the City Center Area, Eight Participants including Cai Zhengyi

Today is the last day to register. It is expected that there will be a fierce competition. The clear records of each athlete are as follows:

The Race Walking Association believes that the refereeing of this pre-selection is of utmost importance. Yesterday, a referee meeting was specially held at Moore Hall. Those present were all experienced in race walking. This pre-selection concerns the national sport. It was unanimously decided to focus on correct posture, average speed, and upright character. Also, for the convenience of the athletes, each athlete must invite one or two introducers to change and advance along the way, and take care of everything.

List of Staff

Chief Referee: Shi Youhui; Secretaries: Lu Yutian, Zhang Jusheng, Yao Yuangan, Liu Yuqi; Finish Referees: Zhang Zao Cun, Li Jiyuan, Chen Yuze, Yuan Qihao; Starter: Yu Zichen; Timers: Wang Fudan, Sun Zhichong, Xu Heng, Zhang Zhihe; Midway Referees: Hou Genren, Qu Guqing, Ai Jieke, Cheng Yi, Chen Niu Zhong, Huang Xiongfu, Wang Zhaoxiang, Cai Songyan, Mao Honggui, Wu Senkang, Shi Ziqing, Le Meigang, Liu Jiajun, Lv Wenxia, Lv Chongyi, Ge Zhonggao.

List of Athletes

101: Li Youren, 101: Cao Guangshi, 103: Xie Xingdao, 104: Qiu Dechang, 105: Wang Jingren, 106: Tan Rongsheng, 107: Cai Zhengyi, 108: Zhang Zaojiu.

The numbers will be distributed tonight. All staff of the meeting are requested to gather at Moore Hall at 12:15 PM this afternoon and take the bus of the Municipal Education Bureau. Latecomers will not be waited for.

Competition Instructions

The competitors must advance on the prescribed avenue and are not allowed to step on the curb. When a competitor overtakes a competitor in front, they must advance at a distance of three steps to the left or right. If a competitor has other reasons during the competition, they may be allowed to leave the designated road, but they must return to the original place before they can advance. The competitors must have their chests straight and their arms free to swing. They must use their heels and toes when striding, but the rear toe is not allowed to be lifted until the front heel touches the ground, and the knee must be straight when the front foot touches the ground (it must be straight when the rear foot is lifted). If a competitor violates the above rules, the midway referee will give a warning and a penalty turn once. The third penalty will disqualify them.

Instructions for Referees

The dispute over the previous 10,000-meter race walking competition is still considered a regret. This time, the World Games Race Walking Preliminaries must be conducted fairly and without any prejudice. This matter concerns the selection of World Games representatives and should not be neglected like the previous 10,000-meter competition. Also, the World Games Race Walking Rules do not allow wearing soft-soled shoes (i.e., rubber soles). It is also hoped that the athletes and referees will pay attention.

Competition Route: The route is the same as the one set for the National Games last year. First, walk around the field for one lap, exit the East Command Platform gate, pass through Guohe Road, Fuxi Nei Road, Huanfu Dong Nei Road, Fu Nei, Road, Xianggu Road, Jungong Road, Zha Road, and Minqing Road to Fufeng You Road, for a total of four laps. Then, turn back to Dong Command Platform gate on the original route via Shanfu Xi Nei Road Guoe Road, and then make one final lap.

China Football Committee Decides Jianmin and Qingxi Will Share the Championship Trophy 217

The two teams will no longer hold a final match

The China Football Committee held a meeting at the Jinlong Hotel at 6:30 PM on the 28th. The committee members present were Jiang Xiangqing (Chairman), Le Xiurong, He Chunhui, Ma Detai (representing Le), Recording Secretary Zhao Kang and Zhang Huijing (acting football association secretary Zhou Jiaqi). The chairman first reported that at the last committee meeting, it was decided that the championship trophy for the Hui Zi group must be determined by a final match between Jianmin and Qingxi. This was originally very fair, but after the decision and the final match schedule were announced, the Jianmin team suddenly protested. The original letter was forwarded by the secretariat, and after further deliberation, the protest letter was not accepted, and the original judgment was maintained. Shen, the secretary-general of the Sports Association, suggested to this committee that before the final match between Gonglian and Zheguang, the Qingxi team's schedule had already ended and that they had already secured the champion position with the highest score, which is to say, Qingxi had already won the championship trophy for the Hui Zi group. No matter the outcome of Gonglian versus Zheguang, it would not affect the already acquired legal rights of Qingxi. If Qingxi requested to receive the awards before the match between Gonglian and Zheguang, the committee could not refuse. Therefore, Qingxi's championship was truly the reward for a season of hard work. Unexpectedly, in the match between Gonglian and Zheguang, Gonglian used unregistered players, which resulted in their disqualification. All past matches between Gonglian in the two cycles were invalidated, and scores were not counted. This move reduced Qingxi's score by four points, while Jianmin indirectly benefited, and their score was one point higher than Qingxi's. Therefore, Jianmin's request to be listed as a champion was also legitimate. To respect the rights and interests of both parties and avoid future malpractices, the committee decided that the two teams must hold a final match to determine the ownership of the championship trophy, which was also the only fair solution to the difficult situation. But now it is no longer the football season, and one of the two sides is still arguing endlessly. It is specially suggested to the committee to judge that the two teams share the championship trophy so that it can be concluded as soon as possible, which is feasible for us, please make a decision. After discussion, it was decided to accept the suggestion of Secretary-General Shen of the Sports Association and ask the Sports Association to add another identical prize to be distributed to the two teams. (Reason) The committee had previously decided that the two teams must hold a final match to determine the championship, which had already confirmed that the two teams had equal qualifications. The decision to award and distribute the championship trophy is still in line with the original intention of the original plan.

Jiangsu Province Normal Middle School Make-Up Exams for Failing Students 218

The Education Department Scheduled Make-Up Exams (Zhenjiang Correspondence) The graduation exams for students of normal schools and kindergarten normal departments this year were held in mid-April. For all students who failed one or two subjects in the previous year's exams, the Education Department has scheduled make-up exams from June 25th to 27th this year. The examination locations are designated as follows: Students from Zhenjiang Normal School, Huaiyin Normal School, and Wujin County Women's Normal School will take the exam at Zhenjiang Normal School; Wuxi Normal School, Taicang Normal School, Suzhou Women's Normal School, Private Jinghai Women's Normal School, Private Jiangsu Women's Vocational High School, and other five schools will take the exam at Suzhou Women's Normal School; Rugao Normal School, Nantong County Women's Normal School, and Private Tongzhou Normal School will take the exam at Nantong County Women's Normal School; Donghai Normal School and Xuzhou Women's Normal School will take the exam at Xuzhou Women's Normal School. Students who have obtained approval to take the make-up exams in their place of service should take the exams nearby in their respective locations. The make-up exam subjects for normal schools are Party Principles, Chinese, Arithmetic, History, Geography, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, Introduction to Education, Educational Psychology, Elementary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, and other eleven subjects. The make-up exam subjects for kindergarten normal departments are Party Principles, Chinese, Arithmetic, History, Geography, Chemistry, Biology, Introduction to Education, Child Psychology, Kindergarten Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, and Childcare Methods, and other twelve subjects. The exam times are: June 25th morning: Chinese, Party Principles; afternoon: Biology, Educational Psychology, Child Psychology; June 27th morning: Physics, Geography; afternoon: Elementary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, Kindergarten Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, Childcare Methods.

Subsidies for Private Schools Under the Control of the Public Works Department 220

Totaling over 220,000 Yuan, Applicants Numbered 244 Schools, Subsidies Could be Used for Awards

Regarding how to allocate this year's Public Works Department (PWD) subsidies of 227,760 yuan to Chinese private schools in the Public Concession, the Education Committee and the Chinese School Subsidy Review Committee have recently held several meetings to discuss the matter. It is reported that a total of 244 Chinese private schools applied for subsidies this year. Among them, 22 schools were deemed unqualified and will not receive subsidies. Of the remaining 222 schools, 46 are new applicants and 176 are previous recipients of subsidies. The Review Committee has recommended to the Education Committee that subsidies be granted to all, with appropriate amounts. The Education Committee, while generally approving the recommendation, felt that the facilities of 24 schools were still questionable and, as per usual practice, reserved them for reconsideration. Subsequently, these 24 schools were individually discussed and decided that one school would not receive a subsidy for the time being. Furthermore, according to the report of the Director of the Health Department, among the schools that previously received subsidies, 147 were considered satisfactory by the Health Department and complied with its regulations, while 30 needed improvement. Among the new applicants, the Health Department believed that 25 schools had the potential to be satisfactory and 21 were considered unsatisfactory. As in the past, schools with improvements in facilities and the potential to be satisfactory may receive subsidies in advance to encourage their improvement. Therefore, the 25 new applicants with the potential to be satisfactory should receive subsidies first, while the 21 unsatisfactory new applicants and 30 old schools will not be granted subsidies for the time being, pending their compliance with regulations and efforts to improve. It is reported that the Board of Directors of the PWD has expressed its approval of the aforementioned recommendations of the Education Committee.

Furthermore, regarding whether PWD subsidies for Chinese private schools can be used to establish scholarships, free student quotas, etc., the Education Committee previously considered it inappropriate. However, the Chinese School Subsidy Subcommittee of the Review Committee recently expressed support for continuing this practice, stating that the PWD's intention in granting subsidies was to assist poor students in general. Currently, the total number of students in Chinese schools subsidized by the PWD is around 46,000, with approximately 4,000 of them receiving free education, accounting for about 9% of the total. Therefore, it is difficult to abolish the existing scholarships and free student programs at this time. This matter was subsequently discussed by the Education Committee, which resolved that items such as scholarships and free student quotas could continue to be included under the subsidy usage items this year for experimental purposes. However, how to ensure that the actual situation and the funds used for these scholarships and free students are used properly still needs to be discussed in detail at the next meeting. The Board of Directors of the PWD has also agreed to the Committee's proposal.

Using Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnity Funds to Establish Sino-Dutch Cultural Institutions 223

The total Boxer Indemnity Funds amount to 2,690,000+ Yuan

The total amount of funds returned by countries such as Britain, the United States, France, and Belgium from the Boxer Indemnity to establish cultural and educational institutions, as well as the repayment period, the institutions established, and other information, have been reported in previous issues. Based on the investigation, the following is an abstract of the table showing the return of the Boxer Indemnity by the Netherlands. The return of the remaining Dutch Boxer Indemnity funds was resolved through an exchange of notes between the Chinese government and the Dutch Minister to China on April 4th, 1933. This exchange of notes is the agreement for the return of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity. The Chinese and Dutch sides then established the Board of Directors for the Management of Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnity Water Conservancy Funds under the Executive Yuan in August of that year. Currently, there are two Chinese directors, Ma Chaojun and Sun Fushi, and one Dutch director, Paul Sowerby. The total amount of the Boxer Indemnity to be returned is 1,429,230.34 Dutch guilders. At an exchange rate of 0.53, it converts to 2,696,661.00 yuan in national currency. The principle of its allocation is that 65% is used for water conservancy projects in China, and 400,000 yuan is designated for the Nanjing Surveying and Mapping Institute. The remaining funds (this fund is managed by a board of directors composed of the Chinese diplomatic representative in The Hague, the president of the Faculty of Arts of the Royal Academy of Sciences of Amsterdam, and the presidents of various universities) are used to reimburse the Dutch government for various advances made in China over the years. If there is a surplus, it will also be allocated to the Cultural Fund. The annual interest income of the Cultural Fund should be paid to the Academia Sinica of China at 53%, with 13/53 of that year's interest used as a subsidy for the Academy's activities and 40/53 used to send Chinese scholars and students to study in the Netherlands. Also, 47% of the annual interest income of the Cultural Fund is given to the Institute of Chinese Studies at Leiden University in the Netherlands. This return of the Boxer Indemnity will result in an annual income of approximately 108,477 Dutch guilders, with the repayment period ending in 1940.

Cotton Yarn: Overview of Yarn Flower Delivery in May: Yarn Reached 19,600 Bales, an Increase of 9,100 Bales Over the Previous Month; Cotton Reached 97,300 Bundles, a Decrease of 34,800 Bundles 235

Regarding May’s Golden Rooster Brand yarn, the opening price on December 2nd of the previous year was 205.4 yuan. At that time, after the implementation of currency paper reform in our country, prices stabilized, benefiting exchange rates. The yarn and flower market situation gradually became peaceful. Following this, the European war spread, the Italian-Abyssinian war expanded, and yarn and flowers worldwide rose together. The local market price followed suit. Securities firms and gold merchants were the first to be dragged in. On December 4th, the highest peak reached 213.4 yuan. Subsequently, with the approach of the end of the year, all parties closed their prices, and warehouse yarn stocks increased daily, reaching 300 bales. The market price turned upstream, falling back to nearly the 200 yuan mark. Until mid-March, with the development of spring sales, the mainland purchased large quantities of spot yarn. At the same time, the Qingdao yarn market jumped wildly, Shanghai Japanese yarn was out of stock, and the selling price soared. General non-industry speculators came out in droves, rushing into the yarn and flower market, absorbing forcefully. The buying momentum was unusually strong, and the market reached 210.3 yuan. Recently, the changes have been significant, and the fluctuations even greater. Market rumors are rife. The Sino-U.S. trade agreement and the government's full maintenance of legal tender credit are firm intentions in many ways. However, sellers, considering the rampant smuggling in the north, tend to sell off. The lowest price once reached 192.3 yuan. Afterwards, a certain party struggled vigorously, dragging in large quantities, and rose again to 200.9 yuan. Finally, due to sluggish yarn sales and excessive yarn stocks, sellers supplied large quantities for delivery, leading to a downward trend. The price fell to 195 yuan at the close, a decrease of 10.4 yuan compared to the opening price. As a result, 19,600 bales remained, a sharp increase of 9,100 bales compared to the previous month. The delivery volume was so huge, a new historical record. The delivery price, calculated based on the last three days, was 197.5 yuan, 5.5 yuan lower than the previous month. The delivered goods included more than 2,000 bales of new code such as 20-count Three Stars, Five Blessings, Jincheng, and Double Deer. The rest were previous yarns, continuing to be delivered. It is heard that the receiving parties were all banks, as well as a certain party. The rest were arbitrageurs at 5,000 to 6,000 bales. The delivering parties were mostly yarn merchants and Deda. The broker license numbers and delivery volume of both receiving and delivering parties are listed below:

The opening price of May’s standard cotton on December 2nd of the previous year was 44.25 yuan. At that time, after the implementation of currency paper reform, finance was stable. At the same time, domestic cotton production was affected by both water and drought disasters, and output repeatedly decreased. People's hearts were firm, and the market price advanced daily towards higher prices. Coupled with the tense European situation and the spreading war clouds in Italy and Abyssinia, U.S. cotton, Indian cotton, and third-grade cotton all turned to high flying in unison. The market atmosphere became even more enthusiastic. On December 4th, the highest peak was seen at 46.4 yuan. Afterwards, as the end of the year approached, U.S. cotton news was bad, and the forward price broke the one-cent mark. Indian cotton White Loch went from 220 rupees to 190 rupees. Sellers were active, and the market price fell in a straight line, to within 42 yuan. However, the banking sector and gold merchants did not absorb it. The market price rose again to 45.95 yuan. Extending to recently, with the rush of cotton flock from various villages to Shanghai for delivery, more than 100,000 bundles were delivered last month. This cotton lacks sales channels. 30,000 bundles continued to be delivered this month. As a result, people were panicked, and the market price tended to go downstream. Principles of Skin Diseases 251

— Editor

(Freckles and moles) are caused by the accumulation of skin pigment in one place. Although the cause is the same, the size varies. The medication is different.

(Acne) contains fat lumps. It is secreted from the skin glands. The skin is condensed and closed. It swells into a small blister shape. Squeezing is not appropriate.

(Eczema) is an inflammation of the skin. It is extremely itchy. The treatment is mainly to remove dampness and relieve itching.

(Scabies) is caused by the invasion of disease-causing insects into the skin. It is most itchy. The treatment is mainly to kill bacteria.

(Burns) The bubble phenomenon is caused by the separation of the epidermis and dermis. There is a feeling of pain. The treatment is mainly to relieve pain and reduce inflammation.

(Chilblains) are caused by the dilation of blood vessels and the congestion of blood. The treatment is mainly to reduce swelling and relieve pain. (To be continued)
