In principle, they should enjoy equal rights, but in the past, men were considered people, while women seemed to be objects, appendages possessed by men. They did not have equal opportunities for education, equal opportunities in employment, or equal opportunities for political participation. There was a clear inequality between men and women.

Since the women's liberation movement began, some women have consciously and actively risen up to demand liberation. They want to be treated as equal human beings and gain the rights they deserve, which are: equal education, equal employment, and equal political participation.

Now, the equality demanded by women has nominally been achieved and the goal has been reached, but the actual achievements are pitifully small! Those who can enjoy equal education, those who can find equal employment, and those who can participate in equal political participation are still only a small minority. What is the reason for this?

The Women's Movement Cannot Have Majority Participation. The main conditions for any movement are: 1. Voluntariness, 2. Majority participation. One's own suffering is best understood by oneself, so one needs to rise up and liberate oneself. Liberation that is not voluntary has no value even if it succeeds. As the saying goes, "Zhao Meng can be honored, Zhao Meng can be debased," which is also very dangerous. The participation of the majority gives the movement strength. If a few people rise up and work enthusiastically, but the majority are muddle-headed, unaware, and do not rise up to cooperate, then it will not succeed. Even if it succeeds by chance, it will not be thorough. The reason why the past liberation movement could not achieve complete success and could not have the participation of the majority is one of the reasons.

Knowledge Is Not Equal. Zhuangzi said, "If the accumulation of water is not deep, then it will not have the strength to carry a large boat." We can know that to accomplish anything and fulfill one's mission, there is no shortcut other than doing well in one's studies and improving one's knowledge and ability. However, the fact that women in the past did not have enough academic ability cannot be denied. The reason why their academic ability was not enough was because men and women did not have equal opportunities for education. As the Western saying goes, "Power that is not sought on the basis of knowledge is absolutely unattainable, and even if it is obtained by luck, it is absolutely impossible to maintain." Therefore, in the women's movement, women must first cultivate their strength, do less empty talk, and strive to improve their knowledge and ability to stand on an equal footing with men. The reason why the past women's movement could not achieve complete success is that their academic ability was not enough, which is also one of the reasons.

Therefore, my conclusion is: To achieve complete success in the women's movement, first, the majority of women must participate and cooperate together; second, women must cultivate their knowledge and ability to stand on an equal footing with men! Otherwise, there will only be the empty name of women's liberation, without the reality of women's liberation!

The Past and Present of "Turkish" Women 263

— Ying Tian

During the time of the Sultans, "Turkish" women were almost completely oppressed under the tyrannical power of men. Every young girl, after undergoing a so-called "perfunctory" education, was considered an adult woman. At that time, they should put on a thin veil on their faces, covering their youthful faces day and night, and no man other than their father and brothers could see their face. Going out was rare. Even if they encountered something important that required them to go out, they would be accompanied by other women. As for the veil, they always carefully protected it, never letting a gust of wind blow it open for strange men to see. Otherwise, it might lead to others pointing fingers: "Hmph! This woman is so promiscuous!"

At home, they just ate and chatted. Except for a few farm girls who worked in the fields with their faces exposed, it was very difficult for almost all women to succeed in doing things in society.

At the age of sixteen or seventeen, it was also the time for them to get married and remove their veils, following the evil traditions passed down by their ancestors to marry a man they had never met. But how pitiful it was! When her husband felt like abandoning her, all he needed was a letter of divorce and two people to prove that he did not need her as his wife. The branch rudder was in that situation, helplessly carrying endless sorrow, quietly leaving her husband's home.

A gentleman from the property-owning class would bring a woman called a Halalk from the slave market home. If the Halalk gave birth to a son for him, she would be promoted to the class called Odalik under his control, and become one of his master's wives. Furthermore, daughters of the aristocratic class during the Sultanate period often married sons of a lower rank. Rarely would a governor's son marry another governor's daughter. From this, one can see the painful life of "Turkish" women at that time. Legally, women had no status, and in the eyes of men, they were equal to a toy. Therefore, in every polygamous family at that time, disputes between wives and concubines were often seen.

However, General Kemal, over the past ten years, has broken through the various obstacles of old habits and created a new order. As a result, the women's issue has been liberated, and the status of women has also progressed accordingly. At the same time, the "Turkish" Republic was established a few years ago. This has transformed an old-fashioned Turkey into one that is similar to European countries.

Women after the reform, "civil servants" that could not be done before, have now been completely overturned: female lawyers and female judges in courts, news reporters in newspapers. In education, they also have the same rights as men to enter middle school and take college entrance exams. Divorce and marriage are also carried out in accordance with the laws of Western countries. At least polygamy and the habit of wearing veils have been completely abolished.

In all new environments, the intelligence and character of Turkish women have been significantly affected. They are absolutely not as bound as they were in the veil era. They actually engage in free love. Other aspects of life, such as everything in the family, have also improved rapidly.

Turkish women are completely in the tide of liberation. It is remembered that in 1932, the Turkish Queen Haunm was elected Miss World. At that time, they achieved a glorious victory in the women's world of the national sports group.

Turkish women are no longer what they used to be. Their improvements are really fast. However, they are always grateful to their Kemal.

Women's Sleep and Other Things 264

— Gao Geng

The morning alarm clock rings incessantly, but the women turn over and go back to sleep. They sleep more than men and sleep more easily and quietly.

Many experts have studied the problem of sleep and dreams. The result is that men mostly have nightmares because they have more work and worries.

They further say that dreaming is not a necessary element of complete sleep, but constant nightmares are a symbol of physical unsoundness. He also believes that seven hours of sleep is enough for people over the age of thirteen.

A rough blanket or even a hot water bottle can cause nightmares. Some very strange dreams are caused by hot water bottles placed under the feet.

We dream very quickly. Events that often take an hour to describe can occur in dreams in just one or two minutes. When we are assassinated in a dream or encounter some frightening event, we wake up and see that it is just the rattling of the window or the banging of the door. Sometimes it is even the ticking of the clock!

The expert suggests that if you cannot fall asleep, you can close your eyelids and focus on the center of your forehead. This is the natural position of the eyes after a person falls asleep. Doing so can clear your mind and gradually fall asleep.

Many great people have the characteristic of sleeping little. The reason why their short periods of sleep can restore their body and mind is entirely due to the pleasantness of their sleep.

This Year Is the 30th Anniversary of the Martyrdom of Pioneer Qiu Jin 265

— Daisy

Ancient Chinese sayings have traditionally regarded thirty years as one generation, and reaching the age of sixty is called a full cycle of the zodiac, which is slightly different from the Western custom of regarding one hundred years as a century, but they can complement each other. The Western saying that one hundred years is a century represents one "life," while the Chinese thirty years represents one "generation." Examining the Chinese translation of the French word Siecle as "century," although it is unknown who created it, tracing its etymology reveals that the French word Siecle is originally derived from the Latin word Saeculum, which means generation. Just as the Latin word Aetas, meaning age, can be understood as one hundred years or thirty years, as in the ancient poem Nuoc terta vivitur aetas, where "three generations" means thirty years as one generation. The poems written by Plautus and Terentius all regarded one hundred years as a generation. The creation and evolution of the languages of the two ancient civilizations of the East and West have unexpectedly coincided. Therefore, our Chinese reverence for modern martyrs and sages can also adopt the saying of thirty years as one generation to replace the grand ceremonies held every one hundred years or twenty-five years in Western countries. Since June of the Dingwei year when the female knight Qiu Jin was executed at Xuantingkou, it will soon be the thirtieth anniversary. If major newspapers in the country can collect anecdotes and poems with a more enduring time scale, it may be possible to designate the thirtieth year as "Qiu Jin Year." Here are two seven-character律詩 poems commemorating Wan Ye Qiu Jin Year, to solicit comments from comrades at home and abroad. The poems say:

Her amazing talent and unique style met the autumn knight,

A beautiful woman who left the world, resembling a sword immortal.

Martyred for the country, she was more virtuous than Xi Shi,

Her earth-shattering deeds are unparalleled by Nuwa's legends.

Sharpening her knife in the Yellow Sea, she sang as if crying,

Boiling blood in Xuanting, her passion seemed to ignite.

Thirty years ago, in this very place,

The vicissitudes of the city and the Jian Lake boat bear witness.

The jade dew withers, and grief is shared with Du Mei,

The cemetery's ice and snow shine with hidden plums.

Achieving benevolence and seeing righteousness are heroic deeds,

Her talent as a prime minister rivals Cang Shui and Wen Shan.

The spirit of nation-building fills the universe,

The flowers and trees blooming early respond to the wind and thunder.

Qiu Jin and Yu Jin are truly unparalleled,

After mourning Zhou Lang, we return here again.

To Women 266

— (Zhao Chen Wanlin)

Do not waste the money earned with your husband's blood and sweat. Do not excessively seek luxury.

Do not be arrogant. Be humble and gentle. Do not despise or insult your husband.

When your husband comes home, show warmth, because he has been working all day and is mentally exhausted. You must make him happy and restore his fatigue.

Always keep the house clean. Do not be lazy and playful, causing your husband to be dissatisfied.

Do not gamble. Do not go to the theater alone. If the family finances are not sufficient, do not complain about heaven and fate, causing your husband to be unhappy.

When handling household affairs, do not listen to other people's opinions. Do not exceed ordinary friendship with men and women, causing your husband to be suspicious.

Special Report of this Newspaper

Interview with Western Painter Ms. Pan Yuliang 267

— Ji Ping

The night before yesterday, I was chatting at Liu Haisu's house and unintentionally talked about several successful Western painters in China. Haisu is truly an artistic rebel. He is very strict when criticizing others. In his eyes, there are simply not many, especially women. We were talking enthusiastically when suddenly a woman in a Western suit came in. That was Ms. Pan Yuliang. She is one of the top Western painters. For the past twenty years, she has traveled all over Europe and Asia and has had special success with oil painting. Probably no one who has seen her work would deny that. That night, I also talked with her for half an hour and learned that her past experiences were very difficult. She lost her husband one month after birth and her mother at the age of eight. She grew up relying on her uncle. She said, "People have loving parents, but I only have kind uncles and aunts." She got married at the age of nineteen, had a child, and then went to Europe to study. The scene of her studying hard abroad back then was also quite interesting. Here, I have written down her conversations in a mixed way:

Artistic Life

I first asked her to report on her artistic life over the past twenty years. She said, "I have always liked art since I was a child. Now I can continue to make a living in the art world and have become a lifelong professional. My courage is very strong, and I have been able to grasp my own aspirations. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, I graduated from the Art College and received a subsidy from Anhui Province to study in France. I entered the Paris Art College, graduated in four years, and learned a little about the field. I then went to the Italian Academy of Fine Arts to study ancient European art. I was the first Eastern woman to study there, so the teachers and students looked at me with different eyes. I was a struggling student, and the provincial funds were in arrears and not paid. Sometimes, only thirty or fifty yuan were remitted, not a round number. I boarded with people and barely paid the boarding fee. I took care of my own meals. Sometimes I bought a few pieces of bread just to fill my stomach. It was unbearably bitter. In my third year of study, I received the Royal Prize of 5,000 lira, which was the first honor in my life. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, I returned to China and served as a professor in the Art Department of Central University for six years. Now, I have accepted an invitation from the Art College to serve my alma mater. In my life, I most like to travel to mountains and rivers, such as Fushan, Jiuhua, Taishan, Putuo, Huashan, Zhongnan, Xuefeng, Tiantai, Yandang, Huangshan, Laoshan, etc. I travel alone and make a living along the way. Over the years, I have created more than 200 works, which are scheduled to be exhibited at the Zhonghua Academic Society starting on June 2nd. Please give me your guidance from all walks of life, both Chinese and foreign."

Urban and Rural Women

Since Ms. has traveled to various provinces, she is naturally very clear about the situation in rural areas. So, what are her impressions of women in urban and rural areas? I asked her this.

"I have always admired the working spirit of European rural women. Over the years, I have walked through several provinces in the north and south and have come to believe that the working ability and thrifty virtues of rural women in our country are actually superior. It seems that there is no distinction between men and women in the countryside. They all operate in the same way, and their physiques are equally strong. Women also have to take care of household affairs. Sometimes, when their husbands go out, they take on all the responsibilities of household affairs and farming. This is something that people in the city cannot match. They only have one regret, which is that they do not have the opportunity to receive education, and their knowledge is too shallow. Their mental abilities are not sharp enough. As for urban women, especially in Shanghai, they are really too extravagant. Excessive decoration wastes time and money, which is a great pity! I am not opposed to it, but I advocate having a certain limit, otherwise, the gains will not outweigh the losses. It always gives people a bad impression. Some things should be done by themselves, and there is no need to leave everything to servants. They must also know themselves, not be delusional, not admire vanity, and reflect on whether my thoughts, knowledge, and integrity are suitable for modern society? Whether my way of dealing with people is beneficial to the public? I hope that today's Chinese men and women will achieve true equal status—" These are her few powerful words.

The Way of Husband and Wife

I also asked her what her insights were on the way of husband and wife. She said, "Between husband and wife, the first thing is sincerity. Neither party can tolerate perfunctory or arrogant tempers. Perfunctoriness can only last for a while, and it can never last. Suspicion is even more intolerable. Often, one thing is hidden, and a gap arises, which turns falsehood into truth, and even the truth becomes false. Conflicts are inevitable between husband and wife. There must be a peaceful attitude. Facts speak louder than words. Concede at the time and explain afterward. What cannot be understood? In some families, economic independence leads to all kinds of drawbacks. Women can accumulate savings, while men are prone to squandering, and even end up losing their wealth and reputation. I advocate economic openness and implementing a family accounting system. Husband and wife cannot live together all year round. There must be several short periods of separation, which is also a way to maintain conjugal love."

Finally, I found a chalk drawing of a fugitive in her bookcase. I stared at this great man. Although he was a fugitive, his spirit was extraordinary. Therefore, I have printed it above.

Fugitive 268

— (Painted by Pan Wangliang)

Postpartum Exercise for Women 269

— Guo Taihua

During pregnancy, the abdominal muscles of the parturient woman are stretched as much as possible due to the enlargement of the uterus; the vaginal muscles are also excessively enlarged when the fetus is delivered through the vagina; the anal sphincter muscles are also enlarged along with the levator ani muscle due to the force exerted during childbirth. Therefore, after childbirth, the abdominal muscles will be permanently relaxed, and the original tension will disappear, or the abdomen will droop downward, the vaginal muscles will become relaxed and enlarged, and the anus will prolapse and incontinence of feces and farts will occur. To prevent the above-mentioned sequelae, the following postpartum exercise method is presented for postpartum women to implement in accordance with the law. The various postpartum exercise methods mentioned below contain the following benefits and functions: 1. They can restore the normal position of the uterus and help the uterus contract and recover; 2. They can restore the tension of the muscles and prevent the abdominal muscles from becoming relaxed and sagging; 3. They can restore the strength of the gluteal and leg muscles and prevent the limbs from becoming soft and weak after childbirth; 4. They can restore the contraction force of the vaginal and anal muscles and prevent the vaginal and anal muscles from becoming relaxed; 5. They can improve the relaxed systemic muscle strength after childbirth, increase the appetite of the parturient woman, and promote mammary gland secretion. Therefore, normal parturient women should implement it in accordance with the law for the sake of health and the beauty of body posture; if the parturient woman has abnormal delivery and postpartum diseases and perineal rupture, the date of starting exercise must be postponed.

Hand Exercise Method: Starting from the first day after childbirth, you can lie on the bed to perform it. For hand exercises, perform it three times a day for three minutes each time in the first week, and four times a day for five minutes each time afterward. When performing it, you must use force on the muscles of the fingers and buttocks.

Uterine Recovery Exercise Method: The best way to recover the entire uterus is for the parturient woman to breastfeed herself. However, the uterus is vagrant, especially during the process of muscle and ligament contraction and recovery. Due to the posture of lying in bed after childbirth, the uterus will change its position at any time. If you lie on one side for a long time, the uterus will be fixed and tilted to that side, forming various uterine displacement diseases. Therefore, you should lie on your back for three hours after childbirth, and then alternate between lying on your left side, right side, and back, with an average rotation. However, each time you turn over, you must be careful and slow, and you must not move or twist suddenly. You must also use your hands to support and press the abdomen and uterus. If the perineum has been sutured, you must first put your legs together when turning over. After three days after childbirth, turn over and lie prone once every twelve hours, for a quarter of an hour each time; starting from the fourth day, add crawling exercises on the bed each time you lie prone; after the fifth day, add the knee-chest lying method as shown in Figure A, because crawling exercises, the knee-chest lying method, and lying prone can all prevent uterine prolapse and have a great effect on abdominal muscle contraction.

Illustration A: Postnatal Knee-Chest Position Method 270

Abdominal Muscle Exercise Method: Two days postpartum, lie supine with legs extended and mouth closed. Use the nose for shallow and deep breathing, inhaling with full force to contract the abdomen, making the abdominal muscles contract and sink as much as possible. Raise and expand the chest, using the power from the lower abdomen (dantian) to inhale deeply. When exhaling, exhale slowly and gradually without using abdominal force. When performing the exercise, place a light bowl or cup on the abdomen. Then, lie on the left and right sides, performing shallow and deep breathing as above, contracting the left and right abdominal muscles. Initially, perform this exercise once in the morning and evening, each time breathing five times. After four days, when performing this method, the supine position with arms and legs extended can be changed to a supine position with knees bent and side lying as in Illustration B. At the same time, increase the frequency to once every six hours. Crawling exercise on the bed: Because the exertion of the chest, shoulders, and hands during crawling naturally causes the abdominal muscles to contract, it is also very effective for restoring abdominal muscles. Starting from the sixth day postpartum, in addition to the above exercise methods, the upper body sit-up exercise method can be added as shown in the figure below, sitting up six times each time, twice a day. Starting from the fifteenth day postpartum, add the standing upper body bend-down exercise method, twice a day, three minutes each time. If the weather is warm, it is best to perform this exercise in sunlight. As for the old method of tightly binding the abdomen with an abdominal binder, it has now been proven ineffective for restoring abdominal muscles and preventing abdominal enlargement and sagging. Some doctors also say that using Aboba Zhunyu to rub the abdominal skin can effectively reduce abdominal skin wrinkles, but this is also inaccurate. Therefore, the restoration of abdominal muscles can only be effectively achieved by performing the various exercise methods mentioned above. However, when postpartum women get out of bed, wrapping an abdominal binder can indeed make the abdomen feel more comfortable.

Illustration B: Knee-Bent Supine Shallow Breathing, Deep Breathing, Contracting Abdominal Muscles 271

Vaginal Muscle Exercise Method: When the fetus is delivered through the vagina, the fetal head excessively dilates the vagina. Therefore, postpartum women should start three days postpartum and automatically contract the vaginal muscles twice every hour, with each contraction lasting half a minute to one minute. In this way, the vaginal muscles can contract and restore, preventing vaginal muscle relaxation after childbirth.

Anal Muscle Exercise Method: Starting three days postpartum, automatically contract the anus once every two hours.

Foot Exercise Method: Start performing this exercise three days postpartum. First, raise the left foot, then the right foot, and then raise both feet together. During the exercise, the toes, calves, and thighs must exert force. However, those who have had perineal sutures must start performing this exercise two weeks later.

Pitiful Northwestern Women 272

— Di Cang

Since Rousseau's "Naturalism" and the concept of "Natural Rights" led to the French Revolution, it indirectly triggered the women's movement. Women in various countries have successively fought for their status. Backward Chinese women, after the first year of the Republic of China, have also made considerable progress in the status of women. But upon closer examination, only a very small number of "Heaven's favored daughters" have enjoyed some superficial liberation. The majority of women, however, are still doing men's playthings, living a miserable life of cattle and horse labor!

Northwestern women, who are in a place where feudal ideas are strong, society is unstable, and the rural economy is bankrupt, are sinking into the deep pit of the old ethics. Foot binding, ear piercing, lack of education, and all kinds of suffering, marriage is still arranged by parents and matchmakers, no different from a kind of salable creature. They have no human status at all. Slaves are brutally beaten by their mistresses, daughters-in-law are abused by their parents-in-law, wives are oppressed and abandoned by their husbands, which is generally considered to be a matter of course. After the death of her husband, she must observe chastity, and tragedies such as suttee and burying young widows alive are commonplace. They themselves also think that this is "virtue". The scourge of the old ethics has ruined many young women.

As for the enjoyment of education and the right to participate in politics and inherit, it is only to create value for the daughters of the parasitic class. The young ladies only know to compete for beauty in school and to compete for favor in front of the opposite sex; once married, they are other people's people, only knowing the "three obediences and four virtues." The hard-working women trapped in the countryside cannot even maintain their own minimum living standards of cattle and horses. How can they take care of these problems? Apart from secretly envying their vanity, they can only lament their own poor fate.

Nowadays, most of the knowledgeable women in the southeast are only intoxicated in the bright lights and green wine of the dance halls, dreaming of being wives and grandmothers. How many are still continuing to work hard, preparing to go deep into the masses of hard-working women, to be their guides and pioneers, to save those women who are living inhuman lives in the hell on earth, to create happiness for the masses of women, and to remember the powerless northwestern women who cannot rise up!

To Sister Fen Staying in Nara, Japan 273

— Xue

—Second Letter—

Fen, I don't know if you have seen the first letter I sent three days ago? What are your thoughts after seeing it? It's best to tell me some.

I don't admit that I am a complainer, but since "returning to the motherland," the complaints in my stomach have really been accumulating more and more, to the point where I have to complain; however, I still don't want to add a layer of depression to you every time you receive a letter from me, so today I am determined to put everything else aside and just tell you a very interesting romantic story, so you can laugh a little.

Aren't I staying at my eldest sister's house? And the room they assigned me to stay in is right behind my eldest sister's own bedroom. Although there is a wall between them, I can still hear all the sounds. The night before yesterday, around one o'clock, I was suddenly awakened by a loud noise. I listened intently and found that it was my eldest sister arguing with my brother-in-law because he has been coming home very late every day recently. This is a very normal thing, who would bother to listen to them. Unexpectedly, the quarrel became more and more fierce later, my eldest sister cried, and Xiao Ling also cried. Then I heard a bang, and my brother-in-law slammed the door shut and stormed out with very loud and rough footsteps.

When things got to this point, someone had to go out and mediate. But before I could get dressed, my brother-in-law had already left through the back door, leaving only my eldest sister and Xiao Ling crying together. It was only with the help of Liu Ma that we managed to stop them from crying. Then, my eldest sister told me with a gnashing expression that my brother-in-law had an affair and was going to live together outside soon, so the family's finances are now very tight, and even Xiao Ling's tuition fees cannot be paid, but my brother-in-law still doesn't care. Finally, my eldest sister announced a countermeasure, which was to file a lawsuit.

Although I am not a supporter of the "litigation is always unlucky" theory, I also oppose creating social news material for the newspapers for the sake of family disputes. Therefore, I strongly advised my eldest sister not to implement her own proposal and promised to come up with a better countermeasure for her.

This sleep was ruined by them! My eldest sister first told me one by one many details that had been hidden, and there were enough words to fill two baskets, but to pick out a few points to clarify the situation:

Seven months ago, my brother-in-law had a romance with a female colleague surnamed Liu;

According to my eldest sister's investigation, although the other party often lives and mingles with my brother-in-law, she is not very frivolous in nature, and her family education is also very strict, so the two have not had any improper behavior;

The other party asked my brother-in-law to divorce my eldest sister first, and then talk about marriage;

My brother-in-law really intends to propose a divorce to my eldest sister. (To be continued)

Talking Points

Aviation to Save the Nation and Dancing to Save the Nation 274

— Nan

Standing in today's world, air defense is quite important. For example, Abyssinia is said to have failed because it had no air defense. Therefore, when they saw Italian planes coming, they had to hide. Although in addition to airplanes, the "importers of civilization" seemed to have poisonous gas bombs to fumigate the "barbarian people" like mosquitoes, in short, suffering from the lack of air defense was still quite a lot.

Speaking of something more personal, then it is best to look at the January 28th Incident. Enemy planes dropped eggs in the sky over Zhabei. With a bang, black smoke rose everywhere, followed by a burst of fire. The common people in Zhabei were naturally crying everywhere, but the concessions were quiet. Quite a few "higher-class Chinese" opened rooms in large hotels to play cards and act as observation posts for "watching the fire from the other side." At that time, the International Hotel did not yet exist. Otherwise, I think it would be even more intimate and beautiful to look down from the International Hotel. Of course, the International Hotel has nothing to do with the "refugees." In addition to making the "fire watchers" happier, the lives and property of the refugees will still be destroyed by incendiary bombs and bombing bombs. However, this is enough to prove that China's air defense is not sound and needs to be well established.

As for dancing to save the nation, that's just a joke. Maybe the person who invented these four words still had a satirical effect. Otherwise, the sound of banning dancing would have disappeared long ago, which shows that dancing is ultimately harmful to "social security and the future of the entire nation." But it's not entirely true. For example, aviation donations are collected by seat in dance halls, but this is of course a profound intention to ban through taxation. Now it is a better method to use entertainment to expand aviation propaganda. Because in this erotic Shanghai, using "hula dances" and other things to appeal will definitely have a great effect. Didn't the previous flood relief entertainment use "flower selection" to appeal? So although the tickets are expensive, people from all walks of life are still eager to buy them, and at the same time, it is enough to see that the people's enthusiasm for supporting the expansion of the aviation to save the country movement is "very good."

Special Feature

Aviation Entertainment Fair at the International Hotel 275

——A Collection of Evening Dresses That Night

Just as our "friendly" strong neighbor was using a huge number of fighter jets carrying five hundred pound bombs to bomb China to death, Italian crow-like planes were bombing Abyssinia into a scorched earth. At this time, our China seems to be waking up.

Workers, elementary school students, and businessmen, they know "aviation to save the country." The power they can do is to save their pocket money, collect a few copper coins, and turn them into a whole number to buy airplanes and donate them to the government. They all have a fire-like heart, although after holding a ceremony, these airplanes are still put aside, but they still deeply believe that their airplanes will one day drive away the enemy.

There are too many things that come out of "aviation to save the country" that have nothing to do with "saving the country." Recently, we have also seen the "Aviation Entertainment Fair" held on the very high skyscraper of the International Hotel.

Naturally, everyone should be happy. In China, where aviation is still quite young, who has a great interest in aviation. I believe that if this aviation entertainment fair was not held on the high skyscraper, but in a wilderness, there would definitely be a large number of aviation-enthusiastic people to enthusiastically participate.

I myself, like other aviation-enthusiastic people, really want to know if the "aviation to save the country" of the non-working class is the same as theirs. They must be shouting in their hearts: "Why is it held on the thirteenth floor? Why are you isolating us?"

"Mr. Li Dachao is not available. He said to give you a few books to read."

"Please return these books. We are not here to read books, we are here to interview for news. Please ask him again, does he entertain reporters?"

That trained attendant number 165 stood still, his face sinking:

"He said he's not available, so of course he doesn't entertain."

"We saw that trained attendant seemed to be Mr. Li Dachao's plenipotentiary representative, rejecting us like that. We wanted our business cards back, and didn't take the books he kindly gave us, and left.

We were thinking, think about it, why did he reject us? Could it be that the "Aviation Entertainment Fair" is just for the entertainment of the higher-class gentlemen? Does it have nothing to do with "aviation to save the country?" Does it not need widespread publicity?

But how can we tell the readers? All we saw were silver snake-like electric lights, red lanterns, black cars, evening dresses, two different faces of trained attendants, and a few yellow-faced books.

If the readers want to know the content of the entertainment fair, then I can only write about it abstractly based on their publicity:

Under the colored lights, on the half-drunk and pretentious faces of the gentlemen, sweat washed away the powder on their faces. Their eyes narrowed, their hands trembled. Many eyes hidden behind glasses, bulging out as if looking at the bare body in the center turning into a flea under the lights, making the gentlemen itch all over...

Readers! Miss ×'s performance of the "hula dance" may be even more moving than what I wrote, or maybe what I wrote is inaccurate? But what method do I have to tell the readers accurate news?

Thinking of this, I felt that it was really necessary to write about the situation of this "Aviation Entertainment Fair" for everyone to see. So, in such a lively mood, I invited reporters from various newspapers to go together. On the way, I had already planned to come back and tell the readers the good news on paper about how many airplanes they had donated.

Very excitedly, I hurried there in the deep blue night. From afar, I saw the tall building of the black International Hotel, with its long string of electric lights, like a fiery red chain. In front of the door, two old-colored red lanterns for weddings were placed conspicuously. This is the Aviation Conference!

The car stopped non-stop at the door, and friends in evening dresses followed behind the evening dresses and went in. Watching them arrogantly step into the elevator, holding the powdered arms of fancy women

Page 22

, when we were about to step in, the trained attendant number 165 of the International Hotel stopped us. We took out our business cards and told him to report to Mr. Li Dachao that we were here to interview for news. The attendant took the business cards and went up, and we waited for a reply on the sofa by the door.

Sitting on the sofa next to us was a Western couple in evening dresses. A compatriot of ours in an evening dress, bending his waist like a shrimp, was smiling and saying fluent English to the Western couple. The perfume emanating from his body, mixed with the unique breath of the Western race emanating from the Western lady's body, made people itchy.

I stood up and focused my gaze on the elevator entrance. The elevator was busy transporting evening dresses. The trained attendant was respectfully treating the owners of the evening dresses with fear of inadequate service.

An elevator brought down the trained attendant number 165 who had just taken our business cards up. He was holding a silver tray with a few yellow-faced books piled on it. He walked up, his face no longer smiling:

On the Songhua River 276

— Ding Li

The sharp wind mixed with snowflakes and ice chips blown from Siberia angrily roared across this lonely night's wilderness, forest, and sparse villages...

Several feet of deep snow piled up on the ground, plump and delicate, looking like it was flowing slightly; the silvery-white color emitted a faint light in every corner of the earth, and this light was reflected on the ink-black sky, just like the thin morning mist in autumn morning, this faint light flowed on this dark wilderness, it replaced the task of the stars and moon to illuminate, so as not to make this rich wilderness fall into the abyss of darkness.

The forest, a boundless forest, stood silently, the huge treetops blurred in the dim air, facing the direction of the wind, the trunk was written with the snowy verses of the far north, it sang of the bitterness in it. Far away to the left rear of the forest, a long mountain range meandered, and the majestic outline was dyed with a layer of blurred thick night, as if it was a little withered, and as if it was about to stand up its strong chest and start a heroic fight with the darkness. Below it was the northern river—the Songhua River.

In spring, in summer, in autumn, (The Songhua River is like a strong child gradually growing into a heroic husband.) It roared and tumbled in the riverbed, it sprinkled tears on the beautiful riverbank, in its heart are buried some sad deeds, the deeds are increasing the record every day, and every accompanying event bites its heart, it is angry, it is sad, it cries, it wants to turn to the sky and pour out the sad record to mankind, it asks for a fair trial. …

Winter, the cold winter in the north, the torrent of the Songhua River is firmly sealed by thick ice, and the sound under the ice is not heard, as if it has been forgotten by people. —The frozen Songhua River has been thickly covered with snow, and it is only slightly different from the ground.

Dogs, a few military dogs, greedily twitched their noses and struggled to pull their legs and run towards the hard riverbed of the Songhua River. Closely following are a few loaded mule carts, swaying their bodies like drunkards from afar, climbing over with difficulty. The snow was brought by the wheels and made a low, muffled sound, and the sound gradually approached.

There were no other movements. Armed soldiers hung their guns diagonally and guarded the car door. The firelight of cigarettes lit up in their mouths. Some were dozing off, and some were projecting sharp eyes from under their leather hats towards the distance. They didn't talk. Not a word, silently waiting for what was about to happen. The dog running in the distance barked from time to time, and the sound seemed to be a little hoarse, as if separated by a layer of fog.

After a while, they (even the dogs) stopped on the Songhua River, and the mules and horses let out a few muffled long neighs. After that, the armed soldiers vigorously jumped onto the car, opened the car door, and dragged down many young people. They: were naked to the waist, blindfolded, gagged, their hands tied behind their backs, and their feet shackled. They staggered and fell to the ground.

The armed soldiers swept away the snow on the ice, and then used iron shovels to dig holes in the hard ice—the roar of the Songhua River rushed out from below. In this sound, the sharp short knives of the armed soldiers slashed at the heads and shoulders of the bound young people, or pierced into their chests and wherever else... The young people bled, they couldn't shout, they couldn't fight, they just trembled painfully and stomped their feet hard.... Then they were thrown into the previously opened hole on the ice and disappeared into the Songhua River. The river water jumped out angrily...

Plop! Plop... The young people were thrown into the arms of the Songhua River with bloody wounds!

As if afraid that the river water would rush out of the hole, the cold froze the hole again, the snow suppressed the blood of the young people, and everything returned to its original shape not long ago, as if nothing had happened....

This, only the Songhua River understands! It embraces, kisses the stiff bodies of the young people with knife wounds with cold lips.

The sharp wind mixed with snowflakes and ice chips blown from Siberia angrily roared across this lonely night's wilderness, forest, and sparse villages...

The earth is gradually tending to be clear!
